3b:["$","p",null,{"children":["The tutorial simulates ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"hadron propagation"}],": starting from the strong-coupling vacuum (a product state), place a meson at the center of the lattice and evolve in time. The differential measurement protocol — running the circuit with and without the central meson, then subtracting — isolates the coherent hadron signal from both hardware noise and boundary effects. The result is a light-cone pattern of fermion density oscillations characteristic of a confined meson breathing mode."],"className":"group paragraph-el text-text-primary mx-0"}]
